<p>Borrowed, likely from French or German. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">a-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:seksueel.html>seksueel</a></i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aseksueel.html>aseksueel</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>asexual, not experiencing sexual attraction</li>
<li>asexual, not procreating sexually, not pertaining to sexual procreation
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">geslachtloos</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>asexual, not displaying sex or sexual dimorphism
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">geslachtloos</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***aspen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aspen.html>aspen</a> (15576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:aspen.html>aspen</a></i>, corresponding to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">asp</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aspen.html>aspen</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:aspen.html>aspen</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:aspen.html>aspen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Pertaining to the asp or <a href = vnd.unilang:aspen.html>aspen</a> tree.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Tremulous, trembling.
<ul><li><b>a. 1631</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Donne" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Donne">John Donne</a>, ‘The Apparition’, <i>Poems</i> (1633):
<dl><dd>And then poore <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aspen.html>Aspen</a></b> wretch, neglected thou / Bath'd in a cold <a href = vnd.unilang:quicksilver.html>quicksilver</a> sweat <a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a> lye / A veryer ghost than I […].</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of a woman's tongue: wagging, gossiping.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:aspen.html>aspen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">æspen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">æspan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">combining form</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">æspe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:aspen.html>aspen</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">asp</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aspen.html>aspen</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">aspens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The asp tree; a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:poplar.html>poplar</a> tree (genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Populus_sect._Populus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Populus sect. Populus"><i>Populus</i> sect. <i>Populus</i></a></span>). A medium-size tree with thin, straight trunks of a greenish-white color.
<dl><dd><i>Above a certain elevation, the <b>aspens</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> way to scrubby, gnarled <a href = vnd.unilang:pines.html>pines</a>.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1912</b> January,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zane_Grey" class="extiw" title="w:Zane Grey"><a href = vnd.unilang:zane.html>Zane</a> Grey</a>,  chapter 8, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Riders_of_the_Purple_Sage" class="extiw" title="w:Riders of the Purple Sage"><a href = vnd.unilang:riders.html>Riders</a> of the Purple Sage: A Novel</a></cite>, New York, N.Y.; London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harper_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:Harper (publisher)">Harper amp; Brothers Publishers</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/6868219">6868219</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>Instead there <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> the white of <b>aspens</b>, streaks of branch and slender trunk glistening from the green of leaves<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title=", and the darker green of oaks, and through the middle of this forest, from wall to wall, ran a winding line of brilliant green which marked the course of cottonwoods and willows">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The wood of such a tree; usually pale, lightweight and soft.
<dl><dd><i>She <a href = vnd.unilang:claimed.html>claimed</a> that <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aspen.html>aspen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the only "proper" material from which make a wicker basket.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:asperge.html>asperge</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">asparagus</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sparagus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀσπάραγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aspáragos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Aspirin</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">acetylierte Spirsäure</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">acetylated salicylic acid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The second word <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> from the name of the plant genus <i class="Latn mention" lang="mul">Spiraea</i>.
</p>

***assistent.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:assistent.html>assistent</a> (2735)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">assistēns</i>, active participle.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:assistent.html>assistent</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:assistenten.html>assistenten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:assistentje.html>assistentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:assistente.html>assistente</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>assistant, person who <a href = vnd.unilang:assists.html>assists</a>, aid</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Often enters as first term in copulative compounds, the second term (after a <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a>) specifying which assistance the person lends or rather who receives assistance.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">adjunct</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">helper</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li></ul>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:assistente.html>assistente</a> (5327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:assistent.html>assistent</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:assisteren.html>assisteren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">assister</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">assistō</i>.

***ast.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ast.html>ast</a> (71151)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:ast.html>ast</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:ast.html>ast</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*astaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:ast.html>Ast</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ast.html>ast</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌰𐍃𐍄𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">asts</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">ոստ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:ost.html>ost</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὄζος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ózos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="cim"><a href = vnd.unilang:ast.html>ast</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b><span class="Latn" lang="cim">éste</span></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sette_Comuni" class="extiw" title="w:Sette Comuni">Sette Comuni</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> conifer branch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="cim"><a href = vnd.unilang:dar.html>Dar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ast.html>ast</a></b> ist guuts holtz so prönnan.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Conifer <a href = vnd.unilang:branches.html>branches</a></b> make excellent firewood.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ast.html>ast</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>

***astrologie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:astrologie.html>astrologie</a> (27782)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:astrologie.html>astrologie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">astrologia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">astronomy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀστρολογία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">astrología</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:telling.html>telling</a> of the stars</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄστρον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ástron</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">star, planet, or constellation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">-λογία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-logía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treating of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, combination form of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">-λόγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lógos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one who speaks (in a certain manner)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">astro-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-logie</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:astronomie.html>astronomie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">astronomia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀστρονομία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">astronomía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄστρον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ástron</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">star</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νόμος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nómos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">law</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">astro-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nomie</i>.
